Central Propaganda Department Hosts the Press

Fang Juehui Reports on Impressions of Traveling in Europe

Yesterday afternoon (the 18th) at 2:00 PM, the Central Propaganda Department hosted the press, inviting over twenty reporters from various Beijing and local Beijing-based news agencies. Secretary Zhang Tingxi presided, extending greetings before introducing Central Committee member Fang Juehui, who reported briefly, stating that all report materials from the trip to Europe were entrusted to a forwarding company and have not yet arrived. Today, he will simply offer a brief report on his impressions from visiting various countries, consisting of five points: (1) The intense patriotism in each country. Every country he visited universally avoids foreign goods. Even the American mail ship from Shanghai to the United States does not purchase foreign goods because all the food

Page 10

supplies used are prepared in their own country. Taking one piece of fruit from Kobe to the United States will incur a fine of fifteen yuan because the American continent is abundant with fruit and does not allow foreign goods to encroach. When switching to a German ship in the Atlantic, all the supplies used on board are German goods. Continental Europe has many small countries, and one can travel through several countries in a day. Everywhere he went, only their own national goods were used. Their methods of resisting foreign goods are all extreme. There are also no foreign goods in the markets of each country. If there are any, they are all subject to heavy protective taxes to show resistance. However, the Chinese stores seen along the way are full of foreign goods; otherwise, they would not be considered stores. What is even stranger is that Chinese silver dollars, copper coins, and banknotes are all printed with English characters. Although this matter is small, its implications are significant and we must pay attention to it. (2) The consistency of diplomatic administration in each country. Traditional diplomats are not used because the political parties and countries in Europe and America each have their own party policies and functions. For example, once U.S. President Hoover takes office, all foreign envoys and consuls are replaced to implement his party's agenda, so he must use the talents of his own party. Mussolini in Italy also uses this method. As for revolutionary countries, such as Turkey, its ambassadors to France and Germany are all wounded senior military officers. This is also a method of implementing their consistent policy. Their revolutionary diplomacy has a specific policy, with not losing national rights as the principle. (3) The restrictions on sending students abroad in each country. European and American countries send students abroad based on the needs of diplomacy, commerce, and various technologies, unlike China, which has no restrictions. Mr. Dai Jitao’s book "On Japan" includes statistics showing that China has sent over 100,000 students to Japan and over 17,000 to Europe and America, totaling over 117,000 people. Provinces and localities all have dispatching offices, and most of the students sent are around twenty years old, with no basic knowledge. After studying abroad for several years, they almost forget their own country and only learn a little superficial knowledge from others. Now China should unify the system of studying abroad, and the central government should decide on dispatching based on the needs of talent. Those dispatched must have basic knowledge before they can study abroad. The state should also be responsible for employing them after they return; otherwise, wouldn't the 30 million yuan that China sends out each year to support students be wasted on foreign countries? The methods used by foreign countries to send students abroad are that the ages are all over thirty or forty, and only after graduating from university and serving for several years with experience can they be sent abroad to study. After completing their studies, they must undergo a training period before they can be officially employed. This is very different from China. (4) The strictness with which each country levies taxes on foreign travelers. European and American countries levy a population tax on foreigners entering and leaving the country. The United States charges eight U.S. dollars per person, Germany six marks per person, and France twenty francs per person. This income is already considerable. There are also passport taxes and freight value certification taxes. For example, if Germany ships goods to Japan, it must be thoroughly investigated by the Japanese ambassador to Germany and a freight value certificate issued, with a tax of one or two percent deducted. China is completely different. There is no population tax. The passport tax has been drafted by the Ministry of Foreign Affairs and is being planned for implementation. The freight value certification tax has never been implemented. If these three things can be implemented, it can generate more than 100 million yuan in revenue per year. Why worry about insufficient diplomatic expenses? This is a sovereign right that our country should have, and there are no unequal treaty provisions, so why worry about not being able to implement it? This is also one of the differences between China and foreign countries. (5) Observations of Soviet Russia. He passed through Russia for more than ten days, but the markets in various places were bleak and desolate. The people on the streets are workers wearing old clothes. Their exclusion of foreign goods is extreme nationalism. Russian workers are absolutely subject to the method of allocating food and clothing to the people. It is said that in 1918, the Communist Party nationalized the land of the large Russian landlords. The land of small and medium-sized farmers was not confiscated. The new economic policy was not determined until 1922. The current five-year economic plan is based on this principle. After the land of the large landlords was confiscated, private serfs became national serfs. All production belongs to the state, and then the state issues small booklets to receive bread and other items. For small and medium-sized farmers, the state collects part of their surplus, just like the method of allocating food between landlords and tenants in China. Food is issued once a day. Everywhere we went, we saw that clothes for receiving bread were issued twice a year. Everyone has extremely little freedom in all aspects of food, clothing, housing, and transportation. All rights are deprived. There are about 50,000 to 60,000 Chinese workers in Russia. These people will never be able to escape for the rest of their lives. To sum up, the above five items are completely opposite between China and foreign countries. This is something we must pay twelve points of attention to. Moreover, as the ancient Chinese books say, "Shame not to be like others is great," and "Cultivate shame." These words are not wrong at all. When I arrived in Sweden from Norway, the money for selling newspapers was left on the street, but no one picked it up because foreigners regard it as a great shame to take what is not earned by their own labor, unlike China today, where everyone picks up money and ignores shame, like robbers. This matter is very important to the national culture, and the education of cultivating shame in a nation is also urgently needed. The meeting was adjourned after the report.

He Jian Will Go to Zhuzhou and Liling to Supervise the Troops

Pursuing the Remnants of Zhu, Mao, Peng, and Huang

Changsha correspondence: After the communist bandits Zhu, Mao, Peng, Huang, etc. secretly left the Changsha area on the 14th and fled towards the Hunan-Jiangxi border, most of their armed soldiers fled from Datuo Shop, Yijiawan, Zhuzhou, and Liling near Changsha to Pingxiang. Only a small portion of Peng and Huang's armed soldiers and tens of thousands of the Liuping Red Guards (all spear teams) fled from Tiaomajian and Yongan City to the Liuping lair. After receiving the report, He Jian immediately convened a military meeting at the headquarters on the 15th to discuss the pursuit plan. Wang Dongyuan, Peng Weiren, Li Jue, Tao Guang, Gong Bingfan, Luo Lin, and others all attended. It was decided to pursue and intercept them separately, and a deadline of the 16th was set for mobilization and departure for separate suppression. In addition to ordering other units to be on alert in southern Hunan and deploying the reserve and reserve teams separately, a telegram was sent to the Jiangxi army to block them. Once the plan was set, Chen Guang's central unit crossed the river on the 16th to Yijiawan and pursued Liling. That night, they camped in Zhuzhou. Luo Lin's unit also departed from the province to Liling early on the 16th and camped in Yijiawan that night. Li Jue's unit reached Tiaomajian on the 16th and decided to pursue Yongan City on the 17th. He Jian, because most of the bandits fled to Liling and Pingxiang, anticipated a fierce battle above Liling and below Pingxiang, so he decided to personally go to Zhuzhou and Liling to supervise the troops the day after tomorrow. As for the whereabouts of the communist bandits after their escape, at 7:00 AM on the 16th, Zhang Yuheng, leader of the 5th Aviation Team, accompanied pilot Yang Xialin on the Dallas No. 2 aircraft to inspect Chen's territory. According to the report to the authorities: (1) About 20,000 to 30,000 bandits have fled from Liling along the railway line to Chudong Bridge in Yidong, and then divided into three routes to Pingxiang: one along the railway line, one from Jinhanchong in the north of the road via Lingguan, and one from Dingjiafang in the south of the road via Fenshui'ao. Their vanguard has crossed Laoguan, and the tail is still in Chuan Chongpu. Their actions are hurried and their order is very chaotic. (2) On the railway at Yingtao Ridge in eastern Liling, there are hundreds of female bandits carrying luggage, following the bandit team. Upon closer inspection, they appear to be cement bags, about 2,000 to 3,000 bags. Several 120-pound bombs were dropped on the densely packed bandit troops, killing hundreds of them. The survivors fled in panic. (2) Two to three hundred bandits in Zhuzhou City fled to Liling in two routes: one along the railway and one from the small road east of Zhutianpu, Shufangchong, and Wen Yijiawan. There are about one hundred bandits heading towards Longtoupu. There are about one hundred bandits heading towards Youmachong on the main road of Tianxinpu and Liumuqiu. The above scattered bandits are all in groups of three to five, in a very embarrassed state. (4) The troops on our southeastern front have advanced with flags, and Laomiao and Langli City have also been occupied by our army. The remaining pursuing troops have all reached their designated locations. Their actions are extremely excited, and the bandit troops are already surrounded. (September 17th)

A Tragic Village Burning Incident by Bandits in Anqiu, Shandong

Jinan Correspondence: The Jiaodong bandits north of the railway currently still include a force led by Liu Yongquan in Guangrao. Liu's unit was originally the Guangrao Garrison Team and is currently negotiating reorganization. The bandit leader Wang Ziming, south of the railway, was originally a remnant of Zhang Zongchang. Gathering over a thousand people, he suddenly attacked Jingzhi Town in the southeastern township of Anqiu on the night of the 12th, setting fires and killing people. For a time, the firelight illuminated the sky, and the sounds of shouting, killing, and weeping could be heard for dozens of miles. This town is famous for producing white wine and is ten times richer than Anqiu City. It has over two hundred militia members, all equipped with firearms. Only sixty people escaped that night, and the fate of the rest is unknown. The villagers came to the province the other day to appeal. The general headquarters immediately telegraphed the 58th Brigade of the 20th Division of the 12th Army stationed in Jiaoxian to suppress them. Yesterday, Zhan's brigade had a fierce battle with the bandits near Songguantuan Village near Jingzhi. The details are unknown. Gao Guizi's Gao Jianbai Brigade, which broke through from Zhucheng, has now fled to the southeastern coast of the city and is being recruited by Shen Honglie, who is sending warships. Gao's unit has not caused any disturbance to the local area. As for Zhang Huizhao's Jin army unit in Wenshang, it is still surrounded by Chen Xiaosi's 2nd Police Brigade. There are no Jin troops south of the Yellow River. (September 16th)

Guangzhou Banquet Merchants Still Suspended Awaiting Decision

Banquet Merchants Request to Self-Manage Banquet Donations

Provincial Government Agrees to Improve Joint Order Penalties

Three Chambers of Commerce to Mediate

Guangzhou Correspondence: Since the Guangzhou Restaurant Association opposed the implementation of joint orders for donation merchants and suspended business, ten days have passed. The banquet merchants have repeatedly petitioned various agencies, but no results have been achieved. The banquet merchants are very determined to oppose joint orders. On the 11th, they again petitioned the provincial and municipal party departments. The party department only agreed to forward the letter to the provincial government for early resolution. In the afternoon, they went to the Finance Department to petition. The Finance Department sent Yang, the third section chief, to receive them on their behalf. On this day, the attitude of the banquet merchants changed slightly, and they requested that if the authorities could not abolish the joint order case, they should return the banquet donation to the Restaurant Association for self-management. Finance Minister Fan Qiwu immediately replied as follows: (1) Explain how the joint order hinders progress so that it can be improved. (2) After the joint order is implemented, more than 800,000 yuan in banquet donations can be collected each year. If the self-management is taken back, an annual quota of 800,000 yuan should be recognized. Afterwards, the banquet merchants returned to convene a meeting. Whether the merchants can pay 800,000 yuan is still under investigation before self-management can be taken back. Now it seems that the banquet merchants have no choice but to rest and await a decision. As for the official government, they do not want to withdraw the order on using joint orders for donation merchants because the funds are involved. They still insist on implementing the original plan and will only make some revisions to the joint order penalties to comply with emotions. This method has already been seen in yesterday's provincial government instructions. The provincial government's statement said (District Jingming and others from the restaurant and tea room association have requested the release of three detained colleagues and the cancellation of the joint order, and the details are known. The Nanjing Municipal Government also has this method of banquet donation joint orders for restaurants to comply with, which is no different. This time, the province's finances should approve the use of the two joint orders, which is not very different. The petition only says that the joint order is difficult to implement and does not clearly point out the difficult facts. How can they dare to suspend business and gather crowds to coerce? The Finance Department has been instructed to reduce the penalties. If there are errors in the procedures and disputes arise, fairness must be maintained. Each of the merchants has assets and capital, and they should all continue to operate as usual and not suffer losses from being incited by others. The government has high hopes. As for Lin Ji and others, they have already been released by the department and returned to business. Let everyone know.) After the provincial government's reply, the City Business and Civilian Association, the General Chamber of Commerce, and the City Chamber of Commerce, three organizations, believed that the unresolved suspension of business by the banquet merchants was affecting the commerce of all industries. Yesterday, they specially sent a letter to the Restaurant and Tea Room Association, instructing them to send people to the Chamber of Commerce to state the situation in order to mediate. (September 14th)

Plague Discovered on the Siping-Taonan Railway

Harbin Correspondence: The news that the plague has been discovered along the Siping-Taonan Railway is spreading. According to a telephone call received by the Eastern Railway Medical Office from Qiqihar on the 12th, the Taonan Railway Bureau received a confirmed report that twelve people have died of the plague in a place eight kilometers from Taonan in the past two days. Also, several people with suspected plague have been discovered in a certain village. Five people have died not far from the South Manchuria Railway along the Sipingjie Railway. The government has now banned people from traveling to the area. The Taonan Railway Bureau has sent doctors to investigate the truth. After receiving the report, the Eastern Railway immediately sent four specialized members of the Medical Office to investigate on the 13th. At the same time, the South Manchuria Railway also issued a notice to rectify the epidemic prevention team and prepare to depart for the three northeastern provinces if necessary. Yesterday, it urgently telegraphed Wu Liande, an epidemic prevention expert residing in Shanghai, to return quickly in order to find ways to prevent the Harbin epidemic. Harbin has experienced two outbreaks of pneumonic plague in 1910 and 1920, and tens of thousands of people died from the epidemic, which is still talked about today. Dr. Burke, a representative of the Health Department of the League of Nations, came to Harbin and talked about how people around the world know that the Manchurian plague occurs every ten years based on past experience. This year is 1930, and I am afraid that the ten-year revival period is approaching. Although his words are not entirely believable, if the plague has recently been discovered, perhaps this saying will come true. Regarding this matter, according to Shi Jiliang, a medical officer from the Epidemic Prevention Office of the Three Northeastern Provinces, the two plagues in 1910 and 1920 were both pneumonic plague, which is easily transmitted through the air and is very fierce, and the area is quite large. This time, the bubonic plague has been discovered near Sitai Road, Pujia Town, Taipingchuan, Kaitong, and Tongliao, where Mongolian villages are located. Fortunately, it is all bubonic plague and will not be as fierce as pneumonic plague. However, more than twenty people have died. The cause is due to the transmission of rat fleas. Rats become infected, and fleas suck their blood and absorb the plague toxin, and then transmit it by biting people, causing the plague. However, after the bubonic plague becomes septicemic in severe cold weather, it turns into pneumonic plague. The Epidemic Prevention Office has sent medical officer Wang Yizhen, along with the Sitai Road medical officer, to do their best to fight the epidemic, and has taken a large amount of serum and plague antibody. If necessary, the epidemic prevention team will also continue to depart. (September 13th)

Strict Prohibition of Tobacco Planting in Northern Anhui

Wei Lihuang Orders All Counties

Violators Will Be Subject to Military Law

Bengbu Correspondence: Northern Anhui is the most famous area for tobacco production. Over the years, the authorities have mostly adopted a policy of concealing the prohibition through taxation, which has only helped to increase drug abuse. This summer, Wei Lihuang, the commander of the Northern Anhui Garrison, was ordered to collect a tobacco seedling tax, which was originally intended to supply military needs for a time. Now that the tobacco seedling tax is about to be completed, it is time to strictly prohibit planting of the poisonous crop. Yesterday, he specially telegraphed the twenty-six counties in northern Anhui to strictly prohibit planting. Violators will be subject to military law. The original telegram reads: Urgent. To the magistrates of the twenty-six counties in northern Anhui: I have learned that opium and drugs harm the country and the people, and this is extremely serious. I have repeatedly received strict orders from the central government to suspend and strictly prohibit this. However, I have found that the counties in northern Anhui have not completely prohibited it. The reason is either that the county magistrates have not made enough effort to prohibit planting or that ignorant and foolish people are greedy for profit. If this is not reduced, production will increase and become a hotbed for bandits, causing great harm and endless poison. This commander is in charge of the military in northern Anhui and is heartbroken by what he sees. Now that the planting season is approaching, it is imperative to solemnly announce and strictly enforce military law. The following items are listed separately: (1) If any county magistrate or township or district chief violates the order or conceals the truth, they will be deemed to have failed to implement the order and will be sentenced to death. (2) If the people disobey the prohibition and still dare to plant, those who plant will be shot and the land will be confiscated. (3) If county magistrates or district chiefs are transferred in the future, they must also be prosecuted according to the law and will not be allowed to escape the law. (4) You are hereby ordered to immediately print 500 copies of the announcement in each county and post them in various townships and districts so that the public is aware of the strict prohibition. You are also ordered to report within one month for record. Wei Lihuang, Commander of the Northern Anhui Garrison and Commander of the Provincial Bandit Suppression. (September 16th)

There is Hope for a Turnaround in the Zhenjiang Market

Jiangbei Station Will Be Moved to Beigushan

Water and Land Trade Can Restore Its Former Glory

Zhenjiang is one of the treaty ports, and its commerce has always been prosperous. After the Jinpu Railway opened to traffic, the situation shifted and trade gradually declined. Furthermore, because the Jiangtan beach was silted up, Jiangbei cargo ships could not connect with Jiangbei Station to load and unload goods. Goods were transferred directly at Huojia Bridge in Yangzhou. The commerce of this port plummeted. Local people discussed relief at the time and agreed on two methods: palliative and fundamental. The former would extend Jiangbei Station to Zhenjiang Customs, and the latter would extend it from Nanmen Station to Beigushan. The Zhenjiang Chamber of Commerce presented the proposal to the central government for adoption. This spring, Liu Weichi, director of the Railway Bureau, was sent by the Ministry of Railways to Zhenjiang to survey the situation. He believed that extending Jiangbei Station to the front of the Customs was completely a temporary solution and not a fundamental method. The plan to extend it from Nanmen to Beigushan was limited to economics and could not be implemented immediately. Later, Gao Zifang sought another way to extend it from Gaozi Station to Jiangbei Station for loading and unloading goods, because the route was short and it was easier to handle through the province. The Railway Bureau already had the intention of prioritizing the easier option. When the business community in Zhenjiang heard about this, they actively fought for it. The Railway Bureau, in view of the decline of the Zhenjiang market, decided that it could no longer withstand the blow and decided to extend the route to Beigushan. However, the funding issue was still difficult to resolve. At the time, the Railway Bureau requested that all construction costs be borrowed from the Zhenjiang merchants at interest and repaid from railway revenue. The Zhenjiang business community believed that the amount was too large and difficult to answer immediately. The matter was shelved for several months without a solution. Now, because the Ma Route from the Provincial Capital of Zhongzheng to Beigushan directly passes through Nanmen, Nanmen Station was expanded on the 15th of this month, and express trains stop at the station day and night to pick up and drop off passengers. Extending the route to Beigushan is likely to be realized. On the afternoon of the 18th, Liu Chengshi, Director of the Car Management Office, Xu Chaoyuan, Director of the Beijing Resident Section, and Tang Bingnan, Director of the Resident Office Section, were specially dispatched to Zhenjiang to meet with Yin Zhiluo, a Zhenjiang-based engineer. (The drawings for setting up a station at Beigushan were drawn by Engineer Yin four years ago.) Chen Zhongying, the director of the Zhenjiang-based section, contacted the Chamber of Commerce. Lu Yu and Liang, both standing committee members, accompanied him to inspect the area around Nanmen Station. They then took a car to Beijing at 7:30 PM. It is reported that Director Liu came to Zhenjiang this time specifically to contact the business community for borrowing construction funds. It is estimated that the total cost will be 700,000 yuan (four years ago it only cost 400,000 yuan). The Railway Bureau can raise up to 200,000 yuan, and the rest must be borrowed from Zhenjiang. If the loan negotiations are successful, construction can begin. In the future, the station will be located east of Beigushan. The collection of freight and all other plans must wait until the Railway Bureau has thoroughly investigated the total amount of trade in customs import and export station transportation and Jiangbei Yangzhou's Cuijia Bridge Tax Office in the last three years before a decision can be made. The Railway Bureau also plans to build a shipyard at Beigushan at the same time to facilitate the berthing of ships. Once this matter is realized, the Daxiaochang area will become the most prosperous commercial area in Zhenjiang.

Local Communications

Songjiang

The Xin Song Min Bao is Ordered to Cease Publication. The Xin Song Min Bao in this city has not been published for long. The external reporter, Chen Chaozhi, has been swindling and cheating, which has greatly damaged the credibility of society. The county party department previously sent a letter of warning, but the reporter even impersonated a public security bureau official and committed fraud. He has been accused and is on the run. The county party department has repeatedly received reports from the public and has decided on the following measures in a standing committee meeting: (1) Transfer the case to the Public Security Bureau to quickly arrest and prosecute Chen Chao. (2) The newspaper's employment of unqualified personnel who swindle and cheat and fabricate news to confuse the public should be ordered to cease publication. If they disobey, they will be sealed up.

Zhelin's Poor Harvest and Autumn Survey Situation. The county government and the finance bureau have both received reports from Zhelin and other places stating that the autumn harvest has been poor and requesting verification. They ordered Clerk Hou to go for inspection. Now, it is reported that Zhelin's second, third, fourth, and fifth districts have experienced hail, and the replanted kapok trees have grown more slowly and only yielded a third of the harvest compared to previous years. Also, Yang Mugen and Xu Guixiang reported that the tenth and sixteenth districts were barren. According to the district chiefs, this was not the case. It is known that Zhelin's poor harvest should be notified to the district chiefs to instruct the township police to create a roster and notify the business owners for re-examination to ensure verification.

Telegraphic Accusation of Corruption in Pingzhen. Chen Zhiwen, the district chief of the ninth district of the county, is a graduate of the second training session. He was impeached for corruption in Pingzhen shortly after taking office. The Pingzhen General Bureau has decided to transfer the case to the county government for severe punishment. Now, Tang Xiuyu and others, representatives of the poor people's group in the tenth district of Cao Yanbang, have telegraphed the provincial and county authorities, stating that Chen Zhiwen, the district chief of the ninth district, has embezzled the poor's grain. They have already telegraphed to accuse him. Now, because the district colluded with local tyrants to divide the remaining grain in order to destroy the evidence, they immediately requested the county party department to send personnel to seize 18 packages in the Zhu family's home and 5 packages sold to the rice shop. It is found that the district chief dared to embezzle the poor's grain and colluded with local tyrants such as Sun and Zhu to divide and occupy the grain, disregarding the hunger of the poor people. He has no conscience at all and should be handed over to the Songjiang County Court to be arrested and severely investigated in order to punish corruption. The case has attracted considerable attention from society.

Suzhou

Appeal of the Case of a Male Teacher Seducing a Female Student. Ge Hong, a teacher at Weiting Elementary School, was sentenced by the local court to two years of imprisonment for the crime of harming the family in the case of seducing female student Hong Xiuying. Ge did not accept the judgment and appealed to the High Court. The High Court has scheduled a hearing for October 3.

Telegraphic Request to Pursue the Nanmacun Robbery Case. Nanmacun in Yanmu District of Wujiang County was robbed by bandits from Daguan Lake on the 10th of this month. The case of 24 robbed shops losing more than 10,000 yuan has not yet been solved. Yesterday (19th), Wu Zhong, the county magistrate of Wujiang, telegraphed the Third District of the Water Public Security Bureau again, requesting that a team be sent to pursue the bandits. After approving the telegram, the district chief immediately telegraphed the fourteenth and fifteenth teams to dispatch teams in separate routes to encircle and suppress the bandits.

Bandits in Dianshan Lake are on the Run. Yesterday, about 400 to 500 bandits from Pudong Gang also fled to the vicinity of Chefang Chenmu in the county, intending to cause trouble. Nie Ziyang, the director of the 12th Public Security Bureau of Chefang, reported to the County Public Security Bureau and reported to the County Government for arrest. After receiving the report, County Chief Huang, in addition to ordering the police chief to lead the police to encircle and suppress the bandits, also telegraphed the Third District of the Water Public Security Bureau to order the team to assist in the pursuit. The district chief immediately ordered Xu Boying, the captain of the eleventh team, to lead the team to rush there. However, when the police team arrived at the location, the bandits fled towards Dianshan Lake.

Wujiang

A Large Batch of Opium was Found in Beiluzhen. The Public Security Bureau of Beiluzhen in the county seized Gu Songlin, a passenger carrying six and a half catties of opium, at the ferry yesterday (17th) afternoon. The person and the goods were sent to the County Public Security Bureau for transfer to the County Government for verification.

Changzhou

Wujin and Cheng County Launch a Large-Scale Bandit Suppression. The Wujin and Cheng County Land and Water Army and Police departed simultaneously at dawn on the 18th to jointly suppress the villages in the border area where bandits were fleeing. The temporary commander-in-chief was Wu Chengren, the commander of the 2nd Regiment of the Military Police, and the deputy commander was Wu Deyao, the county magistrate of Wujin County, and Li Leng, the county magistrate of Jiangyin County. The headquarters was located in the Weitang Security Group. The bandit suppression units on all roads completed their search in each bandit-fled area on the afternoon of the same day. As a result of this bandit suppression, the Wujin team on the left wing captured three suspected bandits, Bao Tingsheng, Bao Rendagao, and Jinhuo, in Baojiatang and sent them to the Weitang headquarters for interrogation. The Jiangyin team on the right wing captured eight suspected bandits, Tao Shanzhuang, Cha Fengli, Wan Ronggen, Xu Xibao, Jiang Xigou, Xu Bingsheng, Gu Rongqing, and Gu Rongjun, and captured a bandit monk named Yuan Lai on Jidun Mountain. Also, Li Leng, the county magistrate of Jiangyin, and Li Zonggang, the director of the Public Security Bureau, captured Ding Xifan, a village chief who colluded with bandits, in Dingjiadan, and captured Liu Fusheng, a kidnapping bandit, and six or seven other suspects in Huangshitou and sent them to the headquarters for interrogation. Those who were not involved were released at any time, and the rest were taken to Weicun by the military police to search. County Magistrate Wu took the Wooden Shell Team by boat to the city that night. The police team and the business association patrol team returned to the city on the 19th.

Local Communications Two

Wuxi

A New Wedding Chamber Turns Into a Tragic Building Collapse: Mr. Wang, a villager from the northern township of Wuxi, married a certain lady from the vicinity the day before yesterday. At about 9 p.m., after the wedding ceremony was completed, male and female guests crowded up the stairs to make merry in the bridal chamber, creating quite a lively scene. Unexpectedly, the floor joists, unable to bear the weight, snapped immediately. With a single crash, the entire floor collapsed, and the bride, wedding guests, and others all fell to the ground below, where they were crushed and injured, and the bridal decorations and items were completely damaged. The bride and guests were quickly rescued and treated for their injuries separately.

Large-Scale Opium Trafficker Yu Lunzhi Arrested: In Yu Lane near Yin Bridge, located in the 16th District (Wan'an City) of the county, there is a notorious trafficker of opium and red pills named Yu Lunzhi. Recently, Sun Jinkui, a villager from Sun Lane in the same district, secretly reported Yu to the county, accusing him of being the mastermind behind a robbery case (Sun's family had previously been robbed at gunpoint by bandits) and requesting that the police be dispatched to arrest him and bring him to justice. After receiving the report, the county government was preparing to send police to the village to make the arrest. However, the Public Security Bureau also suddenly received a secret tip that Yu Lunzhi was involved in opium trafficking. Upon receiving the report, Director Xu secretly dispatched Detective Team Leader Shen Minhua and Detective Tang Yaoting to the village at about 7 a.m. yesterday to arrest him at the address provided. Yu Lunzhi was apprehended in the cocoon market in Yu Lane and immediately escorted to the city to be sent to the county government for interrogation.

Private Salt Ship Seized at Wutang Gate: Wutang Gate in Kaihua Township is an important passage to Taihu Lake. The waterway is complex and notoriously dangerous. The other day, dozens of private salt ships were suddenly discovered there, arriving in a large group. At that time, the patrol boats of the Third Squadron of the Seventh Anti-Smuggling Brigade and the Gao Patrol Team were passing through the area. They immediately reported to headquarters and gathered more than 50 patrol boats to surround the smugglers. Under the command of Dong Songyuan, Deputy Squadron Leader of the Third Squadron, and Huang Zhenou, Captain of the Gao Patrol Team, the patrol boats bravely launched an encirclement and suppression operation. After an exchange of gunfire, the private salt ships could not resist and threw their salt into the lake, scattering in all directions. As a result, two salt ships and dozens of bags of private salt were seized near Daijia Village and have been escorted to the city for Director Wu Hanzhuang of the brigade to handle according to the law.

Opposition to Taking Over the Labor Hospital: The Ministries of Industry and Commerce and Health, recognizing Wuxi as a region with developed factories, have specially designated it as an industrial and health zone, dispatching personnel to organize a Health Promotion Association to specifically handle workers' health matters. They also ordered the Labor Hospital to be taken over and reorganized, and an order has already been issued to the county government to assist in the matter. After receiving this news, the County Party Consolidation Committee believes that the Labor Hospital was originally managed by the Industrial Consolidation Committee. If the Health Promotion Association takes over, it would not be in line with legal principles and facts. Therefore, it has been submitted to the committee for discussion and resolution: (1) Send telegrams to the Central and Internal Party Departments, the Provincial Party Department, and the Provincial Government, explaining the original situation and requesting that the original proposal be canceled. (2) Jointly organize a Labor Medical Education Management Committee with the county government, labor, and management representatives, and task the Civil Training Committee with drafting simple regulations. (3) Send a letter to the county government for reference. The above resolutions have already been recorded and sent to the county government for reference and implementation yesterday.

Petition to Severely Punish Private Sellers of Inferior Silkworm Eggs: Silk cocoon broker Yang Zhongjian recently sold silkworm eggs at Wanfeng Silk Cocoon Company. However, the goods were of poor quality and high price, and villagers have repeatedly raised objections and filed a complaint with the county government. Recently, Yang again entrusted a Mr. Li of the railway station baggage room to ship more than 1,000 sheets of inferior silkworm eggs from Shanghai. Coincidentally, Tao Zuiliu, the director of the baggage room, discovered this and immediately reported to the stationmaster, who handed over all these inferior eggs to a technician from the Sericulture Suppression Office for examination. Furthermore, Xu and Xue and others have also filed a petition with the county government to severely punish Yang and others for defrauding villagers of money with inferior eggs.

Changshu

Robbery of Rice Cargo Ship in Kuncheng Lake: Qian Yuxu, a villager from Chuanxin Jing Township in Xiangcheng District, Suzhou County, is a moderately wealthy man with a 21-year-old son named Dingyuan. The night before last, he hired a boat to transport 12 stones of brown rice to Changshu for sale. Unexpectedly, at about 4 a.m. the next morning (the 18th), as dawn was breaking and the boat was passing the Panjiazhakou area of Kuncheng Lake outside Xiaodongmen, it was suddenly encountered by a bandit boat with six or seven strong men. They boarded Qian's boat and searched it thoroughly, finding nothing. As a result, they robbed half of the brown rice on the boat and abducted Qian Dingyuan. However, when they realized that Qian had no money to be redeemed, they released him and then disappeared into the lake. By then, it was already broad daylight. Qian then sold the remaining four or five stones of rice at the Henghe Rice Shop in Fanjiashi outside Xiaodongmen before returning home.

Wangshi Town Receives Another Threatening Letter: Wangshi Town in the mountain area is located on the coast and has been repeatedly subjected to robbery. Therefore, those with some property in the town have been moving to the city. Recently, the market in the town has become even more deserted. The four kidnapped victims who were released last month. Now, the town office has received a threatening letter from An'ang Port in Northern Jiangsu demanding 90,000 yuan to ensure the safety of the entire town. This was noted in this newspaper on the 2nd of this month. Now, the town office received another letter on the 12th of this month, stating that the previous ransoms for the kidnapped victims were too low and they had specially written to request a certain amount of money to be prepared for negotiations in order to ensure the peace and tranquility of the town. Otherwise, they would return to sweep and rob the entire town within ten days. After receiving the letter, the authorities are paying special attention to defense matters and are implementing a curfew every night to prevent attacks.

Jiangyin

Suspicious Points Surrounding the Suicide of Miao Wencai: Miao Wencai, the acting director of the Shengang Public Security Fifth Branch, committed suicide with a pistol just one day after taking office. Upon hearing this, Director Wang of the Police Academy sent Ma Yiyong, a squad leader, to Cheng to investigate, raising various doubts. A special request was made to the county government for investigation. The other day, County Magistrate Li summoned the branch secretary and police officer Fu Xueni, police officer Quan Shoufu, police officer Cao Fusheng of the Nanwai First Substation, Miao Wencai's elder brother Yougang, Wu Bingjun, and others from the Public Security Bureau to the county for interrogation. Ma Yiyong stated that there were many suspicious points surrounding Miao Wencai's suicide: (1) The county did not conduct an examination at the time, which was a mistake. (2) The position of the bullet was incorrect. (3) The wounds were different. If it was suicide in bed, there would be no bullet holes in the wall or curtains behind the bed. (4) The bleeding was incorrect. In short, Wencai was shot to death in his sleep, and the gun was placed beside him. Fu Xueni and others claimed that Wencai committed suicide. Miao Yougang also presented several points of view. After the interrogation, County Magistrate Li instructed Ma Yiyong that the case was currently under investigation. After returning to the province, the various doubts should be submitted in writing to the county in the name of the Police Academy Alumni Association for further study. Fu Xueni and Jin Shoufu were suspected of involvement in the case and were handed over to the Public Security Bureau for detention.

Nantong

Bandits from Tong and Rugao Return: Shen Guanxi, a bandit leader from the ocean area of Tong and Rugao counties, led more than 800 men to Yancheng and Funing to join forces with Ma Yuren. Recently, Shen sent another group of more than 200 men led by Zhou Yuting back to Lvsi, occupying the Sanchazhen District Office on the 18th. A telegram was sent to the county government for emergency assistance. County Magistrate Zhang requested the Eight Counties Bandit Suppression Command to dispatch troops to suppress the bandits.

Recovered Soldiers Prepare to Return to Their Units: Over 1,100 officers and soldiers who have recovered from their injuries at the Nantong 31st Rear Hospital. General Headquarters is assigning Shao Weihan to lead a platoon from the Garrison Brigade to Nantong to handle the discharge and return of the wounded soldiers to their units. Each wounded soldier will receive a return-to-unit allowance of three yuan to prepare for their journey.

Gaoyou

Reporter Sentenced to Imprisonment for Smoking Opium: Min Shiji, a reporter for the Gaoyou Min Guo Daily, was arrested by the Public Security Bureau for smoking opium due to cerebral cold and sent to the county government. Yesterday (the 16th) afternoon, Hu Chengren opened a court session to interrogate him. He admitted without dispute that he smoked opium due to cerebral cold and was immediately sentenced to one month of imprisonment.

Record of the Interrogation of the District Chief's Extortion Case: Wu Kai, the former chief of the Eighth District of Gaoyou, was jointly accused by Zou Chang Shen Maonian, a village head from Yufu Township, Shen Dejiu, a village guard, and Wu Yucheng, the head of Manyang Township, of extortion and intimidation in a complaint filed with the county government. Yesterday (the 16th), Hu Chengren opened a court session to summon the plaintiffs, defendants, and witnesses for the plaintiffs, Chen Shuchun, and the witness for the defendant, Xu Tinggui, to appear in court for interrogation. According to Shen Dejiu, on August 10th, the district chief summoned me and asked me who was posting the "Yellow Oriole" notices. I said I didn't know. Finally, he gave me three days to hand over the person who posted the "Yellow Oriole" notices. On the night of August 14th, the district chief ordered the district guard to call me and said that the district chief wanted to talk to me. Because it was late, I said to the district guard, "It's late tonight, I'll see the district chief tomorrow." After the district guard left, three or four district guards came again and arrested me and took me to the district office to ask if I had found the person who posted the "Yellow Oriole" notices. I said I hadn't found him. He said I was disobedient and inefficient, so he ordered the district guards to tie me up and take me to the Zhenwu Temple in Fan [unclear] for detention. Later, my uncle Shen Xingyuan and the heads of Yufu Township, Shen Maonian, and Manyang Township, Wu Yucheng, negotiated with him and settled the matter with 50 yuan. When he was released, District Chief Wu opened a court session and had me sign a statement. According to Shen Xingyuan, Wu Yucheng, Shen Maonian, and the witness Chen Shuchun, when we went to Fan [unclear] to negotiate with District Chief, the district chief wanted 100 yuan to release Dejiu. Later, Xu Tinggui, the uncle of the district chief, mediated and reduced it to 50 yuan, which was handed over to the district chief at the counter of Xu Tinggui's shop. According to the defendant Wu Kai, Shen Dejiu was in collusion with the bandit Chen Xuemeng, who was wanted in Xinghua County, so I ordered the district guards to arrest him and send him to Fan [unclear], intending to send him to the county government from Fan [unclear]. Later, Zhang Qixin, a police officer from the Fan [unclear] Public Security Bureau, mediated and told me to release him first and give him 20 days to hand over Chen Xuemeng. As for them saying that the money was handed over to me at my uncle Xu Tinggui's house, that was not the case. I only spent one night alone at my uncle's house that night, and they did not go there. According to the witness Xu Tinggui, no money was handed over at my house, and I don't know any of the plaintiffs. Wu Kai did not come to my house that day either. According to Chen Xuemeng, I am 59 years old, a farmer from the Seventh District. I am really a good citizen. I have relatives with Wu Kai. He falsely accused me of being wanted in Xinghua County. I request the court to send a document to Xinghua County to investigate. If there is a case in which I am wanted, I am willing to be shot. I have no enmity with him. Why did he pull me in when he was sued by others? I don't know any of the people in the plaintiff's group, and I have never been to Yufu Village in my life. After the interrogation, the judge ordered both parties and witnesses to sign a statement. Wu Kai and Chen Xuemeng were released on bail with reliable commercial guarantors pending further investigation.

Jiaxing

Resolutions of the County Construction Committee: The Jiaxing County Construction Committee convened an important meeting of various committee members the day before yesterday, and the following resolutions were made: (1) To prepare a budget for the collection and expenditure of public welfare donations from residents along both sides of Xinma Road, and to formulate collection methods, as ordered. It was resolved that official agencies such as the Fire Brigade should also donate funds for public welfare, and that the County Party Department, County Government, County Court, etc., which are all located on Xinma Road in front of the county, should also be subject to the same collection in order to promote it. The remaining residents and shops should be sorted separately to ensure that the burden is evenly distributed and not biased. (2) To establish a memorial tower for the seven martyrs, the names of those who have not yet returned the previously issued donation booklets should be verified, and the booklet numbers should be handed over to members Lu and Wu to collect them. At the same time, member Sheng should estimate the cost of labor and materials according to the drawings, and then invite workers to build it. (3) The third phase of the demolition of the city wall and road construction plan has been approved by the Construction Department and will begin bidding and construction immediately.

Shaoxing

Road Construction After Demolishing Streets: After the Construction Bureau surveyed and implemented the demolition of streets in Shaoxing City, the section from Dajiang Bridge to Qingdao Bridge has been more than half demolished and will soon be completed. Regarding the road construction methods, considering that the commercial residents have suffered great losses due to the reconstruction of houses, it is difficult to bear the road construction costs. The Construction Bureau has discussed in detail and proposed to first complete the construction of the sidewalks on both sides. The streets are planned to be repaired on the existing stone roads. Once commercial development takes place, road construction will be carried out. All road construction expenses will be estimated by the Construction Bureau and submitted to the Construction Department for approval.

Pinghu

Bandits Rob Villages: At midnight on the 14th, more than 20 bandits suddenly broke into the home of Zhou Furong, a farmer near Bozi'an, about three miles southwest of Xincang Town, and plundered at will. They tied up Furong and Da Adi with ropes. However, Da Adi broke free of the hemp rope while being carelessly guarded, attempting to escape. The bandits noticed and pursued him. Angered by this, both Furong and Adi were severely beaten. Furong's left arm was broken, and Adi's head was slashed open. Both were seriously injured. The bandits looted for about an hour before leaving in a huff. According to Furong, the bandits all spoke with local accents and did not have formal firearms.

Huzhou

The Gao Family in Tangqiao Village Robbed: Gao Shunmao, a farmer in Tangqiao Village near Lushan Town, Changxing, is known for his diligence and frugality, and his family is relatively well-off. At about 10 p.m. on the 24th of this month, more than 20 bandits suddenly arrived, speaking with a Hakka accent. They broke down the door and entered. Gao Shunmao and his younger brother Chunmao and others knew that something was wrong and all hid, allowing the bandits to search and loot all their clothes and silver coins. Before leaving, the bandits left a letter instructing Gao to quickly prepare 2,500 yuan, otherwise they would set fire to the house.

Peaceful Express Bus Robbed En Route: The Chunmao and Gongji express buses heading from this city to Heping set off from the city one after the other at around 17:00 yesterday morning. While passing the Miaozimenkou area near Yuantong Bridge outside the West Gate, it was noon. The Chunmao boat was in front when four bandits holding wooden toy guns and speaking with a Henan accent were seen on the bank, shouting for the bus to stop. The bus had to stop. Two bandits were stationed on the shore to keep watch while the remaining bandits boarded the bus and searched it at will. All the foreign letters inside were robbed, and many items brought by the shops were also robbed. Each passenger was searched by the bandits in turn, and no one was spared. After the robbery, the bandits remained hidden on both sides of the Zhaimen. When the Gongji bus passed through the area at around 1:00 p.m., it was also robbed in the same way.

Xiaoshan

Robbery Occurs at Nanmentou: The home of Du Chenglin, a resident of Nanmentou, Xiaoshan, is considered to be moderately wealthy. He usually goes out to do business, leaving only women at home. Yesterday (the 16th), five bandits suddenly entered the house with long poles, first tying up the women with ropes and ordering them to remain silent. They then ransacked the boxes and chests, looting extensively for about an hour before opening the door and leaving. It is said that the loss of clothing, soft goods, and cash amounted to about five or six hundred yuan.

Ningbo

Fire Injures People: At about 9 p.m. last night, a fire broke out at Zhang Shunji's carpentry shop across from Tengjia Lane on the north bank of the city due to a cigarette butt being left in the wood shavings. The fire was quickly extinguished. However, Lao Wang and his wife, who sold barley pancakes and lived upstairs, jumped out of the building one after the other upon hearing the alarm. Lao Wang was seriously injured and was immediately sent to Jiangdong Lu Yinhua Surgery for treatment. His wife, Mrs. Wang, suffered minor injuries and is not in serious condition.

Xuzhou

Commander Yao Reorganizes His Troops: In order to reorganize the administrative personnel, the Anti-Rebellion Army Xuhuaihai Guerrilla Headquarters is implementing a purge. It has dispatched cadres to secretly investigate whether the military brigades under its command are engaging in deception. Commander Yao Zhidao is deeply concerned that his troops may occasionally harass the local population and cause trouble, so he is conducting strict and secret investigations. He welcomes people from all regions to secretly report any such facts so that he can punish one as a warning to a hundred.

Investigation of Public Housing for Establishing a Court: The Jiangsu Higher Court instructed Gangshan County yesterday that it has decided to establish the Third Higher Branch Court in the county, with an attached local court to hear first-instance civil and criminal cases. All matters related to the location of the court are important and should be located in advance to ensure progress. County Magistrate Yang Wei has begun investigating this matter today.

Letter

Letter from Lu ChengZhang and Wang Shushen in Pudong

Regarding the item in the Suzhou Communications column of the local news section of your newspaper on September 18th, titled (Investigation of the Two Hui Collusion and False Accusation Case). The case of Wu Hansheng, the owner of the Hengmian Tongsheng Paper Shop, being a reactionary, was reported by Shao Kangjun, the principal of the Minyi Elementary School near our town, to the local Fourth District Second Branch on August 11th, claiming that he was suspected of being a reactionary. The Fourth District Second Branch immediately forwarded the request to the Public Security Bureau for strict attention. The Public Security Bureau believed that he was indeed suspicious and ordered a chief police officer to go to the store at 8 p.m. on the 12th to search for and find reactionary publications, which were sent to the county and then to the High Court for handling. This is completely inconsistent with what was stated in your newspaper (Luchang Zhang and Wang Shushen, etc., from the Hengmian Town Tongsheng Paper Mill in Nanhui County, owed the store several tens of yuan for paper materials. The store owner Wu Hansheng asked Lu Wang and others to collect them, and Lu and others claimed that they had misrecorded the accounts, causing a conflict). It should be corrected. Lu Cheng Zhang and Wang Shushen, September 19, 19

Educational News

Important News

Ministry of Education Commends Donations for Promoting Education

The Ministry of Education issued a second-class certificate to Zhan Jijilei from Tonghua County, Liaoning Province, for donating more than 5,200 yuan to build the school building of the Second Elementary School in the first district of the county. Also, Zhan Jiapeng, a citizen of Guangde, Anhui, was awarded a third-class certificate for donating 3,000 yuan in cash to found a junior high school in the county. Dong Shougeng was also awarded a first-class certificate for donating 11,000 yuan to found a junior high school.

Ministry of Education Orders Provinces and Cities to Report

Survey Statistics Form for Secondary Schools

In order to investigate the status of secondary education in the country in the 18th year and prepare statistics, the Ministry of Education issued two types of survey forms yesterday and ordered all provinces and cities to fill them out and submit them to the ministry within two months. The original order stated that the status of secondary education in the country had been investigated up to the 17th year. Now, two types of secondary school survey statistics forms for the 18th year have been prepared. One is based on a school as a unit, and each school fills it out on its own. The other is based on provinces and cities (cities under the direct jurisdiction of the Executive Yuan) as a unit, and each province and city hall and bureau compiles a summary table based on the various types of secondary schools. Both tables have attached instructions for filling out the forms. In addition to distribution, a certain number of secondary school survey statistics forms and instructions for filling out the forms, as well as a certain number of secondary school survey statistics forms and instructions for filling out the forms for provinces and cities, are attached. The halls and bureaus are ordered to order all public and registered private secondary schools that were previously distributed to fill out and submit the forms within a time limit. Then, the halls and bureaus will compile the secondary school survey statistics forms for each province and city and submit them to the ministry together with the sub-tables for each school. It is essential that they be submitted to the ministry within two months from the date of receipt of the documents. This order includes the issuance of a certain number of secondary school survey statistics forms and instructions for filling out the forms, and a certain number of secondary school survey statistics forms and instructions for filling out the forms for the Education Halls and Bureaus of Province and City.

The Education Division of Jiangsu selects achievements from the Expo.

Recently, the Jiangsu Provincial Office of Education received a letter from the representative office of our country participating in the Expo in Belgium. I should share any concerns with the participating institutions, and the institutions and schools have pledged their support. If all are donated to the Belgium Government it will add quite a bit more influence to the Education Division of the schools in this province.

The Economic society of China will open its annual meeting today.

The site will be at the Wuxi County Chamber of Commerce

Cai, Dai, Shao and others to give speeches at the meeting

The 7th annual meeting of the Economic Society of China is scheduled to begin on the 20th of this month at the Wuxi County Chamber of Commerce for four days.

Pre-Meeting Arrangements

The venue will be on the upper floor of the County Chamber of Commerce, and arrangements are currently underway. A paifang (decorative archway) with the words "Venue of the 7th Annual Meeting of the Economic Society of China" is erected at the entrance. Next to the train station, a huge colored bamboo cloth is tied with the words "Welcome to the members of the Economic Society of China". The reception place for members is set up in the stationmaster's office in the station and is furnished by Station Master Liu Guangyao. He ordered the arrangements to be ready on the 18th so that the members from various places can sign in temporarily after getting off the train at the venue.

Jinan University Emphasizes Moral Education

The National Jinan University's emphasis on moral education has been reinforced since the beginning of this semester. In addition to establishing a Moral Education Department specifically for the university, a joint moral education committee was also established in conjunction with the middle school department. Tang Demin, former executive committee member and standing committee member of the Shanghai Special Municipal Party Headquarters, was specially appointed as the director of the Moral Education Department of the university. Pan Hua and was appointed as the deputy director, and Rao Shu, Zhang Shaoliang, Guo Shuliang, and Chen Zhongfu were appointed as moral education officers. Xu Minyi was appointed as the general affairs officer, Zhou Canhuang as the dormitory manager, Xie Shengshun as the postal and telecommunications manager, and Xiao Yehui as the documentation officer. The position of chairman of the joint moral education committee of the university and middle school department is concurrently held by Tang Demin, director of the Moral Education Department of the university. Six articles of the joint moral education committee regulations have been formulated, placing extreme emphasis on moral education.

Junyi Middle School Plans to Build New School Buildings

Junyi Middle School, founded by Wu Kaixian, an executive committee member of the Shanghai Municipal Party Headquarters, and others, has been keen to manage its internal facilities and administration since Shen Gongzhan became the principal last semester. In the joint examinations organized by the Municipal Bureau of Education, the school's performance surpassed previous results. As a result, the school became overcrowded in the following semester. This was partly due to the inadequacy of the school's buildings, but also partly due to the strict discipline of the school. It is reported that the school, recognizing that many applicants for admission this semester were turned away, has found it necessary to actively prepare to build its own school buildings. Preparations are currently underway, and it is expected that the school will have a new look by this time next year.

Proposals for the Joint Conference of Vocational Guidance Organizations

The Joint Association of Vocational Guidance Organizations of China is scheduled to open at 2:00 PM on the 21st of this month. Representatives have been nominated by 47 organizations. Today, the following representatives were additionally nominated: Central University (Shen Hongchen), Jiangsu Provincial College of Education (Yu Shoumei), Nanjing Women's Vocational School (Guo Yangyuan), and Zhenjiang Chamber of Commerce Vocational Introduction Agency (Hu Jianchun). The proposals put forward by various parties include: (1) When vocational guidance organizations in various locations encounter difficulties in vocational introduction and vocational surveys, they should seek practical cooperation and mutual assistance to increase convenience. (2) It is recommended that vocational guidance organizations in various locations should jointly study guidance methods to increase work efficiency. (The above were proposed by the Nanjing Municipal Bureau of Education and the Nanjing Vocational Guidance Institute.) (3) Vocational guidance centers in various cities and counties should mutually recommend and entrust vocational personnel. (4) Letters should be sent to public education centers in various counties to add vocational guidance departments. (The above were proposed by the Wuxi Vocational Guidance Institute.) (5) This meeting should be established as a permanent association, and a general meeting should be held in the capital on a selected date. (6) The location, date, and permanent address of the general meeting of this association should be determined. (7) This association should elect a preparatory committee for the general meeting. (8) Standard procedures or steps for vocational guidance centers to implement guidance should be established. (9) Standard procedures or steps for schools to implement guidance should be established. (10) Standard forms for vocational guidance applications should be established. (11) The minimum level of organization for vocational guidance organizations should be established. (12) The constitution of the Joint Association of Vocational Guidance Organizations of China should be drafted. (The above were proposed by the Shanghai Vocational Guidance Institute.) (13) Should this association consult with the Vocational Education Society to hold regular meetings? (14) How should this association publish publications? (15) Should this association organize an executive committee? (The above were proposed by the Wuxian Vocational Guidance Institute.) (16) Secondary schools should increase the number of free places to provide relief to generally out-of-school youths. (Proposed by the Jiading Vocational Guidance Institute.) (17) How should public schools guide the public's occupations? (18) Public education centers and farmer education centers should make vocational guidance their main undertaking. (The above were proposed by the Jiangsu Provincial College of Education.) Additional proposals will be recorded later.

Various Schools Exempt Shaanxi Students from Tuition and Fees

The Shaanxi Fellow-Provincials Association in Shanghai, due to the severe disaster situation in their home province, felt that the students studying outside were greatly affected, and their daily lives were also difficult. Last month, they organized a petition delegation to go to the capital to petition the Ministry of Education, requesting that the Ministry order various schools to exempt tuition fees to maintain their studies. This was previously reported. It is now known that the various schools have received orders from the Ministry to exempt this year's tuition and miscellaneous fees. After receiving the order, the various schools have also tried their best to show compassion. The current Law and Politics, Guanghua, and Minzhong schools have exempted tuition fees and a small number of miscellaneous fees. Law, Fudan, Chizhi, and Zhonggong schools have completely exempted tuition fees. Daxia, the Academy of Fine Arts, Dongya, the Physical Education Academy, and other schools need to have their school affairs meetings resolve the matter. It is heard that these schools have always been committed to nurturing talent, and with the severity of the Shaanxi disaster, there should be no problem with exempting tuition fees.

Japanese Bridge Requests Educational Funding

The Bureau of Public Works Cannot Agree in Practice

The Education Society said that the Japanese expatriates in this city are striving to develop Japanese expatriate education. Previously, the union of various roads jointly submitted a petition to the Bureau of Public Works, requesting that it provide subsidies to the schools and education enterprises established by the Japanese to promote development. It is now heard that the Bureau of Public Works has frequently expressed sympathy in principle, but it is not easy to do so in practice. Because if the Bureau of Public Works grants the Japanese expatriates' request and subsidizes Japanese expatriate education, the Chinese, who account for the majority of the population and taxpayers in the concession, will inevitably rise up and demand that the Bureau of Public Works will have no way to cope. Therefore, although the Bureau of Public Works is sympathetic to the Japanese expatriates' request to develop education, it is actually very difficult to provide subsidies.

The Chinese Expedition Football Team is Scheduled to Return to Shanghai

Due to Procedural Errors, the Expedition Was Suspended

Expected to Arrive Here on the 29th

The Chinese expedition football team's ambition to conquer Europe and America with their strong players is commendable. However, due to procedural errors, the expedition was unfortunately suspended, and the team is now planning to return to Shanghai. Before leaving the country, the expedition team should have submitted their amateur status certificates to the Chinese National Sports Advancement Association, and then the association should have consulted with the South China and other sports associations to invite strong players, so that the team would have strong strength and legitimate status. Other problems could also be easily solved. However, this was not done, resulting in the British side inquiring about the matter with various sports associations in Shanghai and Hong Kong without receiving a satisfactory reply. As a result, the British side refused the team's entry. The Chinese expedition football team's grand plan has become a pie in the sky. Yesterday, someone received a telegram from a player on the team, saying that the team will leave Singapore in a few days and is expected to arrive in Shanghai on the 29th of this month.

Two Organizations Echo Liao Zhang Qiaodian

Promote Peace and Complete Unification

Urge Yan and Feng to Relieve Military Power

Municipal Chamber of Commerce Telegram The Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce yesterday issued two important telegrams on the current situation, which are recorded as follows: (1) To Nanjing Central Party Headquarters, National Government Chairman Chiang, Shenyang Commander Chen, all Headquarters, all Commands, all Military Divisions, all Brigades - We have read Commander Zhang's clever telegram advocating for an immediate ceasefire to alleviate the people's suffering. All follow-up matters will be under the Central Government's direction, etc. The benevolent words benefit all. Peace is precious, as the ancients said. Since the military campaign began, the people have been displaced and the soldiers have died in the fields. All these sacrifices are our people. The Central Government's campaign to quell the rebellion was not originally intended. If all parties have regrets, the Central Government must be benevolent. It is hoped that after Commander Zhang's clever telegram is issued, the Northwest and Jin-Ji generals will repent their past mistakes and work together for peace. They should immediately send a telegram expressing their sincerity. All measures and methods will await the Central Government's decision. Rescuing this turbulent situation and maintaining unification is of utmost importance. We must rely on the people's will to achieve good governance. We await orders. Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce. (2) To all Provincial and Municipal Chambers of Commerce, Bank Associations, Money Trade Associations, Trade Associations, Organizations, and Newspapers - We have sent a telegram stating (telegram as above). The Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce sincerely hopes that abundant harvests will bring prosperity, and that ending the war will bring peace to the people. Seizing the right timing to seek harmony, washing away the war and seeking construction, the opportunity for change is fleeting. It is imperative that all organizations and newspapers unite to form public opinion, promote peace, and complete unification. The future of the country depends on this. The Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce.

The Preparatory Committee of the Shanghai Special District Citizens' Union.

Finance Minister Song Continued Meetings Yesterday

Reportedly Planning a System-Wide Tax Consolidation Issue

The Meeting May Not Conclude in One or Two Days

Finance Minister Song Ziwen convened a meeting at the Shanghai Office of the Ministry of Finance the day before yesterday to discuss important financial matters. According to financial sources, the meeting continued yesterday and may not conclude in one or two days. Minister Song personally attended. The Case of Recovering Concession Telephones Is Transferred to the Ministries of Foreign Affairs and Communications for Planning

The Ministry of Communications Replied to the Chinese Users' Association Telegram

The Chinese Users' Association of the Shanghai China and Foreign Telephone Company received a clever telegram from the Ministry of Communications yesterday stating that the Ministry has learned of the Association's presentation on September 10, in which the Association pledged to defend the recovery of concession telephones to the end, demonstrating its support for national rights and respect for laws. The Shanghai Public Concession Bureau has already signed a franchise agreement with the newly organized Shanghai Telephone Company. The Ministry believes that the clauses contained in the agreement all infringe on rights and violate the contract. The Ministry has submitted a detailed description of the negotiations, listing the points where the contract is not in compliance, and has requested that the Executive Yuan review the matter and determine the method. The Executive Yuan then resolved at its 83rd meeting to hand over the matter to the Ministries of Foreign Affairs and Communications for joint consultation. The Secretariat transferred the letter to the Ministry, and the Ministry sent personnel to consult with the Ministry of Foreign Affairs many times. The government decided to proceed from a practical perspective, first recovering the telephone assets of the former China and Foreign Company in Pudong, South Market, Zhabei, and other Chinese areas. At the same time, the Ministry of Foreign Affairs will actively negotiate the issue of police power in road construction beyond the boundaries. Once resolved, the Ministry will take over the telephone assets in those areas. As for the telephones in the concession, other appropriate methods will be developed to continue negotiations. This plan has been jointly submitted by the Ministry and the Ministry of Foreign Affairs to the Executive Yuan for approval and gradual implementation. The Ministry has ordered the Shanghai Telephone Bureau to estimate the materials needed to convert the users in the Chinese areas of Pudong, etc., so as to purchase and distribute materials and commence construction to take over as soon as possible. The Association is a Chinese users' organization, and it is hoped that the Association will inform the users of the above plan and assist in its implementation. In addition, if there are other effective methods that the users themselves can implement, it is hoped that everyone will work together.

The Water Price Increase Case

News from the Bureau of Public Works

Expresses the Need to Maintain the Original Proposal Yesterday's newspaper reported that Mr. MacNaghten, Chairman of the Bureau of Public Works, replied to the Real Estate Association regarding the water price increase, saying that the Bureau of Public Works will reconsider the matter soon. The reporter of this newspaper visited the Bureau of Public Works yesterday. According to the authorities, the proposal to increase the water price by 40% due to the impact of the gold standard on silver prices was originally passed by the Bureau of Public Works. Although the opposition from all sectors is rampant, the Bureau of Public Works is well aware of the difficulties of the water company, so it has decided to allow it to increase the price. The Bureau of Public Works' current attitude is to maintain the original proposal, and the price increase will be implemented starting this month.

Letter Requesting Inspection of Net Profit Numbers The Shanghai Chinese Ratepayers' Association and the Shanghai Real Estate Association both received letters from the Shanghai Waterworks Company yesterday, stating that (we respectfully request your association to select members and organize a delegation to inspect the net profit numbers on which this company's proposed increase in water surcharges is based) (the Ratepayers' Association) (the Real Estate Association) has also been invited separately in another letter. For the convenience of inspection, we would like to request your delegation to visit our company's office and inform us in advance of the names of the representatives and the date and time of the inspection. It is heard that the Ratepayers' Association is scheduled to hold an executive committee meeting on the 22nd, and the Real Estate Association also plans to hold a meeting to discuss countermeasures.

Foreign Shipping Companies in Shanghai Adopt an Austerity Policy

Dull Business, Layoffs

Chinese Employees Laid Off, Unemployed

The shipping industry this year has been the most sluggish due to the turbulent situation. Suspensions of operations and layoffs are becoming increasingly common. The unfavorable phenomena in the foreign shipping industry are recorded as follows:

Dara The American Dara Shipping Company is a king in the Pacific shipping industry, with 17 giant ships in operation. This year, due to excessive competition with British and Japanese shipping companies, business has been dull. Recently, ships weighing 10,000 tons often import and export only 300 to 500 tons of cargo. Mr. Dara, the owner of the company, is scheduled to come to China on October 3 for inspection. To reduce expenses, a layoff was held yesterday in the Shanghai office.

Five people belonging to the ship's head office have been laid off, and 20 people have been laid off at the Balianjing Wharf. The previous practice of two people managing one warehouse has now been changed to one person managing two warehouses. Twenty-five Chinese people lost their jobs and livelihoods in one day. Each of those laid off was paid three months' salary.

Dalian The Shanghai branch of the Dalian Steamship Company has received a telegram from the head office stating that due to poor business in various locations, austerity measures must be implemented. It has been agreed that a total of 100 employees will be laid off from the branches in Shanghai, Tianjin, Qingdao, and Japan. The president of the Shanghai branch has discretionarily decided to lay off five Chinese employees, and two Chinese employees have also been laid off at the Huangpu Wharf. Only one Japanese employee has been laid off.

NYK After nine new ships were built this year by the Japan Mail Steamship Company, the business was not good, resulting in 140,000 tons of empty ships being docked. The Chinese sailors on each ship were dismissed and sent back to Shanghai and Hong Kong. It is now proposed to reduce the number of land-based office personnel. It is heard that the Shanghai branch plans to lay off ten Chinese employees. The president of the branch has gone to Japan for consultation, and there is also news that the Chinese employees of the wharf police station will be laid off. The implementation will be announced after the president returns to Shanghai. The Osaka Shosen Kaisha has also proposed layoffs.
