Yarn and Cotton: Optimistic Situation in the Yarn Market

Long Positions Adding... Short Positions Covering... Japanese Yarn Rebounding

Upward... Market Very Tight

The sharp rise in the yarn market and the tight situation are due to optimism about the current situation. Therefore, people's hearts are suddenly strengthened, and the upward trend is fierce. Scattered short sellers are again showing panic, so buyers seize the opportunity to purchase and add to their positions, making the market extremely tight for a time. There is a lack of sellers in the market. In the afternoon, due to exchange rates, third-grade yarn also rose by two or three yuan. There are also large accounts covering their positions, but it is said that British factories are also selling short a lot. The subsequent developments still depend on the actual situation for advance and retreat. The current market situation is chaotic and inconsistent, and the market is fluctuating between ups and downs.

It is said that in these few days, various Chinese and foreign factories in Shanghai have pre-ordered about 30,000 to 40,000 pieces of Indian and American cotton. Domestic cotton business is relatively scarce, but factories are purchasing to adjust the color and blend of local cotton, though the quantity of bales is very small. Therefore, although the yarn market has suddenly risen due to optimism about the situation, the cotton market is still flat. The Japanese Dongmian and Han groups are still selling in the standard market. However, with recent spot activity, people's hearts are more stable.

Han Biao (Han Label) Continues to Rise by 0.01-0.02 Taels: The Han Biao market opened with a flat situation. Because the yarn market rose, it was pulled up, and prices rose by 0.005-0.015. The market was still flat in the afternoon. Because Indian cotton prices were cheap, there were still few buyers, and prices rose by 0.01 in each month. The total trading volume for the day was 47,100 dan. Ruidi sold 5,000 dan, Hehua 2,100 dan, Public Tai 2,900 dan, Yuanda 2,500 dan, Yiyu 2,400 dan, Yichang 1,600 dan, and Shenchang 2,600 dan. The remaining amounts were between 900 and 1,000 dan. Lichang bought 4,200 dan, Tianchang 2,200 dan, and Hengde 2,500 dan. Other amounts were between 1,000 and 1,100 dan. Food

Hexia Rice Market Flat and Weak

New Xian Rice Declines Sharply

Zhabei Yesterday, No. 13 and 14 boats arrived at Hexia. Sales were not very good. Although broken Geng rice was dull, there were still some scattered goods being resisted. Therefore, the situation was stable. The price for West New Geng rice opened at 20 yuan and 8.5 jiao. The price for East New Geng rice was also 20 yuan and 5.6 jiao. Central Guan goods gradually softened slightly. However, the market for New Geng rice will be difficult to maintain if the weather continues to be sunny. The market has already turned, and it would not be surprising if it falls back. New Yangjian rice suddenly declined sharply, falling by 0.5 yuan. It is necessary to top it up specially at 15 yuan. The left-hand side of Guan's new Duzi Xian rice fell by 0.6-0.7 jiao. At noon, the particularly high price only opened at 16 yuan. Over 30 truckloads of new Kejian rice arrived from Yuanda. Although sales were still active, the trend was to shorten it by 0.3-0.4 jiao. The highest topping price was only around 14 yuan. The Jiaobaijian market was also sluggish, with the price勉强开 opening at 17 yuan. At the moment, various new Jian rices have all reported fatigue, and the source is increasingly being transported by merchants who are very eager to sell, which is the opposite of the situation when it was sold at a high price in the past. Therefore, Geng rice will be more affected in the future because the inventory is weak and all parties have great intentions to enter. Therefore, high-priced goods hovered between 19 yuan. However, medium-grade goods are inevitably slightly softer.

South Shanghai The source from Hexia is still not surging. Sales on this street are also flat. The focus of transactions depends entirely on the situation in the Zhabei market. Therefore, the arrival and sales here are both weak. For example, it is impossible to see the receipt of broken Geng rice, and only medium-grade Su Tong goods are available. The market has consistently hovered between 19 yuan and 8-9 jiao. The situation is extremely sluggish. Although the new Geng rice and Xiang rice from the city and countryside of this port have not arrived in large quantities, they can already be seen sporadically. Particularly high prices are 20 yuan, and ordinary prices are between 19.5 and 19 yuan. The overall situation is flat. The New Dujian rice market reported poor performance, with the high-priced goods on this surface only opening at 14 yuan and 3-4 jiao. The new Yangjian rice is only 14 yuan, and the selling is sluggish. The market has a continued weakening trend. The factory's new Jian rice has little rise and fall due to cost considerations. The price opened at 13.5 yuan. There are times when it changes and times when it stops. The market lacks standards. High-priced goods are at the 19-yuan mark.

Flour Market Amid Peace

North Sales Hopeful... Market Slightly Rebounds Firm... However, Foreign Atmosphere Still Poor

Yesterday, after the flour market opened in the morning, the prices of various months generally showed a hovering state. In the morning, foreign wheat only had a slight drop of 0.1-0.2 jiao. The selling pressure from the short side stopped slightly or even engaged in covering, so the market felt slightly settled amid the weakness. However, the lowest-end distant months had a slight rebound of about 0.01. When the market opened in the afternoon, it was very optimistic about the situation, and the sales in the north may be able to turn around from this point. Therefore, people's hearts were relatively stable in fact, and the distant months also rebounded slightly. However, the subsequent rise and fall will ultimately depend on changes in foreign exchange. If the exchange rate rises daily, the order of foreign wheat will inevitably be cheaper. This is the most noteworthy thing. As a result, this month was unchanged, October was better by 0.01, November was better by 0.0025, December was unmoved, January was better by 0.005, and February was unmoved.

Wheat Market Amid Rising Exchange Rates

Factory Selling Pressure... Subsequent Steps Still Depend on the Weight

Yesterday, after the wheat market opened in the morning, the atmosphere of declining prices in various months remained unabated. Because the quoted price of foreign wheat also slightly dropped, the comparison of exchange rates also gradually increased. According to the pricing of foreign spot wheat, the settlement with 41 yuan of U.S. dollars only totals 4.7 taels of Shanghai yuan. Therefore, inland factories and small and medium-sized factories in this port still consistently put selling pressure, and the quantities were very large. For example, November saw the lowest price of 4 taels and 6 jiao, and December saw 4 taels, 6 jiao, and 0.01. It seemed that domestic wheat was perhaps not worth much because of foreign wheat. Later, because part of the shorts covered, the market turned stable. Until the afternoon, all plates were set with the situation in the north. Powder sales were set and active, so people's hearts turned more stable. As a result, the difference was small. It is estimated that this month was better by 0.01, October was weaker by 0.02, November was weaker by 0.02, and December was weaker by 0.01. January and February were weaker by 0.02. The attitude of each factory in the spot wheat market seemed to turn active. The high-end goods in each grade did not rise or fall. Medium-grade goods were about 0.01-0.02 yuan weaker. It is estimated that 12,000 bags of Yaowan white and red wheat, Niuzhuang wheat, Shan wheat, and white wheat were opened. Fufeng and Fuxin handled 7,000 bags of Niuzhuang wheat.

North and South Goods

New Quan Pao Longan Second Batch Arrived

The first batch of the New Quanzhou dried longan opened in the market as scheduled due to the large number and moist condition, but the loss was very high based on the cost. However, it was also unavoidable. It was heard yesterday that the second batch had arrived on the Yuanan ship. The amount was greatly reduced, with only 1,200 boxes, which was less than half of the previous batch. If the condition is dry, there should be hope for a recovery. It was also heard that subsequent batches will temporarily stop shipping to Shanghai to promote a turnaround in the market.

Silk and Tea

Hangzhou's New Cocoon Trial Reeling Results

Reeling Loss is High... General Pull Requires 800-900 Catties

The autumn cocoons in Hangzhou this year have suffered from weather damage, resulting in a poor harvest and poor cocoon quality. New cocoon samples from Linping, Yuhang, and other places have been shipped to Shanghai Dingyuan and other factories for trial reeling. The results show that a general pull requires 800-900 catties of dry cocoons to reel one dan of silk.

Zhenmei Green Tea Sales Slightly Active

Yesterday, Lu Zhuang and Tu Zhuang's Zhenmei and Xiumei green teas were started to be handled by Jinlong, Xiehe, Yihuo, Tongfu, and other firms. However, the selling prices were still low. Zhenmei green tea still showed a tendency to increase and then lower prices. Large group teas have become increasingly sluggish in recent days. The current inventory is no less than dozens of groups, making it difficult to sell. Only Yihuo Foreign Firm bought more than 100 boxes of Qimen black tea. The selling price also fell by more than 10 taels.

Piece Goods

Piece Goods Market Amid Progress in the Current Situation

North Group Handling Appetite Improves Suddenly... Over 500 Pieces of Coarse Cloth Transacted

Local Cotton Cloth Yesterday, the market trend turned hard, because the times had developed greatly and peoples hearts were suddenly upheld. The first north was formed into movement. Groups in Tianjin, Niuzhuang, Dalian, and other regions, transacted over 500 pieces of coarse cloth yesterday. The Hubei Tianzi brand rose to eight taels, and sixteen pound double elephants and five old men were also being handled. The searching vigor of small inclined brands from Ningbo and Wenzhou and other regions were rekindled, so they became even more firm. The demand for only fine cloth and coarse cloth was the strongest. Over 100 pieces were received yesterday. White flannel was also purchased daily.

East and West Piece Goods The market situation rose again. The demand from Tianjin groups was very large. The fine serge of East goods rose by 0.025 to 0.05. Huxinting was resold at 0.02675 taels, Hanshan Temple at 0.0265 taels, and Dingfacai at 0.02625 taels. Jian Gongduan rose by 0.025. Feima Tong Queqiao Hui was also sold at 0.02825 taels. Tianjin groups purchased in large quantities. The Han group transported over 200 pieces of Moganshan Jian Gong Ni at 0.03125 taels, Tianci Caiyuan at 6.4 taels, and Four Scholars Jian Gongduan at 0.03 taels. The price of goods seen on this street rose again, and they were added one after another, which was a great difference from the market air of the previous day.

Book and Newspaper Introductions

The Revolution of Love

— Yang Shaozhi

A Five-Act Play, Written by Hu Chunbing

An era has its own literature, and a nation also has its own literature. When a nation evolves to this era and is inspired by the torrent, it will naturally reveal the material of this nation's literature in this era. [Whether a country's national character is understood is greatly related to its country's literature; whether an era is understood is also related to its era's literature.] This is what Lafcadio Hearn once solemnly said. What is the situation in China now? What kind of consciousness does China need? To put it bluntly, China has long embarked on a period of suffering, and most of the people are saddened by suffering and tend to be decadent and depressed. At present, there is a glimmer of hope, which is the recent discovery of a fierce new force in the literary world, radiating an unusual light in the cloudy and dense sky, marking the banner of saving the Chinese nation from disaster. This is something worthy of our joy and elation.

We know that literature is the torch of the nation. Burning it can stimulate national thought and intensify national emotion. In China in an era of suffering, in the morbid state of the decadent and degenerate Chinese nation, we should naturally shake ourselves up, burn the torch of the nation, stimulate national thought, and intensify national emotion. The literary world has seen the crux of the problem, knowing that the era of wagging our tails, begging, wailing, and weeping has passed. If we want to save China, if we want to save the Chinese nation, the only way is to make ourselves healthy. "The Revolution of Love" is a literary work containing such a mission.

"The Revolution of Love" is a five-act play. It is entirely set against the backdrop of the current era, depicting the rampant reactionary forces during the rise and fall of revolutionary emotions. The idea that the Chinese in the eyes of so-called imperialists cannot even hum a tune is written so delicately and profoundly. But it does not dryly and completely depict this kind of all-out revolutionary drama. It takes this as the central consciousness of the play. In addition to attacking the deceptive and despicable behavior of imperialists, it also attacks the old concepts in the old society, and even more so attacks the old concepts and old forces from the reality of love, leaving them completely scarred and without any room for lingering.

The story in the play takes Zhong Sanmin as the protagonist. Zhong Sanmin is a young man with rich reason and emotion. He is extremely firm and courageous, and his mind is extremely precise and profound. He also has revolutionary emotions. However, his father is a very docile foreign slave, taking the comprador in the foreign firm and the foreign manager as emperors. All the characters in the Zhong family, except for Sanmin, have the same mindset as this head of the family, even his relatives. This can be regarded as the result of so-called "matching social status" in Chinese marriage customs.

There are twenty or thirty characters in the play, but each has a special style and can represent the characteristics of the transition period between the old and new societies. Yun Song and Yun Gui's frivolity and boldness, Lei Ma and Zhu Er's prudence and loyalty, Ai Hua's liveliness, and Fang Zi's unrestrainedness further set off the freedom of the Goddess of Liberty. Liberty everywhere forces out the truth and rushes with bravery and enthusiasm. Such a colorful play is really rare in our country's original plays.

In the plot of the first act, Sanmin is absolutely not tempted by profit and lust, betraying his integrity. He knows that the trend has reached this point, and he can fight a desperate battle with the representatives of imperialism. Seeing that Sanmin, in order to seek the success of the revolution, disregards his father's job and the family's income, he even scolds the foreign manager, Addison, saying, "I know that you capitalists who have been officials and warlords are representatives of imperialism. You must know that if we want freedom, we are not wagging our tails and begging for your favors. We are taking back our due rights from your mistakes. If you hold on to our due rights and refuse to give them to us, then we will recognize that imperialism is always imperialism and can only be overthrown!" Such a brave spirit is naturally worthy of promotion. In the second act, he also passionately shouted, "I deeply feel that to overthrow imperialism and the comprador class, we must engage in national revolution and first overthrow the warlords and bureaucrats, so I resolutely joined the revolutionary army to engage in the most front-line revolutionary work." At the same time, in this play, the despicable behavior of the representatives of imperialism is reflected everywhere, which can naturally complement each other and easily remind people's ideas.

However, this play can also be said to be a record of love, but it is not like general works depicting love, focusing on the decadent kind of tune. Although this play has plots about love in every chapter, it still keeps in mind the main central consciousness everywhere. He demands the permanent victory of love. He feels that "I think if I love freedom, I should break away from my family. If I love freedom, I should eliminate the power of the warlords. If I love freedom, I should overthrow the imperialists. I am continuing to work hard for freedom!"

— (Hua Photography)

There are many more good points about this play. Asking my pen, which is not accustomed to introductions, to introduce it would really bury its original brilliance. Please let the people who study literature appreciate it for themselves. In short, I think this is a play of the era. It is completely set against the backdrop of the current Chinese era and takes a proper consciousness as the center. The only thing we see in China, which is suffering from a shortage of modern plays, is imported goods, which naturally cannot cater to the psychology of Chinese audiences. Especially imported goods cannot ignite the torch of the Chinese nation, stimulate national emotion, and fight for the nation. Therefore, the value of this play lies here, and the value of this book being introduced lies here. We know that this year is the year of drama. The public performances of Shanghai spoken dramas are considered to be numerous, but most of the time, our feelings are disappointment. Among them, only the Xin You's Difficult Drama Movement can barely give the audience a kind of strength, making them believe that they have hope if they are willing to work hard to improve. But I still feel that there is a lack of clear and proper consciousness, and the fundamental problem is naturally because of the lack of plays. Now that we have developed such a play, I hope that people who are enthusiastic about the literary movement will work hard to try it.

Book Year Garden

Night

— Shuying

In the night, no matter how dark it is, there is always a kind of radiance. The radiance of the night is extremely gentle and profound, like a silent friend. He comes and gives you warm friendship in silent opposition. Night not only gives people rest, but also gives you comfort.

When the afterglow of daylight has completely disappeared, your heart does not think about past events, nor does it ponder the future, but simply accommodates all the impressions before your eyes—and who has not had such a situation? Whether you are a busy businessman, an artist, a hard-working worker, an official, or a soldier who has just not heard the roar of gunfire, at this time you are as if you have just woken up in good weather, with the warm and gentle rays of the sun and the sound of birds blending together by your side. Your spirit is fresh and keen, and you seem to feel everything for the first time, but without surprise or special love and hatred, you purely accept them with inner feelings. At this time, you can recognize everything at the bottom of the night.

There is a lamp on the table. This may be an electric lamp, a kerosene lamp, or an oil lamp from ancient times. In any case, it is a kind of small-powered bright thing. No matter how bright the lamp is, let's say you hang a 200-candlepower gas-filled electric light bulb in your room, but the light will never be enough. You always feel that outside the window, his face is tightly贴贴against the glass window, with the eyes of the night闪闪shining with gentle and profound light. Even inside the room, the lamplight is just a stranger who has come to an unfamiliar house. No matter what he thinks in his heart, he will run around, but there are always too many omissions. In the corner of the room, beside the table and chairs, on the sides of all the furniture and utensils, near your hands, nose, and ears, and between your eyelashes, the night quietly waits there. As soon as he can come out, he immediately walks out silently, just like a wife who is too docile, always gently serving you beside you, seeing if there is anything you need her to do. Even the beacon fire when Agamemnon triumphed and the spring lanterns of the Lantern Festival in Lin'an can never drive the night away. He will never leave and will always stay by your side.

Different lights have their own special mood. Electric lights are of course the brightest and most convenient. Electric lights give you a lively and warm mood, stimulate your emotions, and increase your interest, but sometimes they make you feel empty, flat, gray, and dim. Electric lights, such as street lights and lights in the kitchen, evoke extreme loneliness and horror. Gas lights are probably the worst. They stimulate you like a commercial advertisement. If you want to read a book, not for entertainment, nor like a scholar quoting extensively, but to quietly appreciate the meaning of the book, or if you are writing something, not with the intention of becoming a writer, but wanting to sincerely express your feelings, then you should use a kerosene lamp. The kerosene lamp never stimulates your light, but only tightly adheres to the circle of light that surrounds you, just as you need it. Outside are some kind darkness that will soothe your thoughts. The kerosene lamp also scatters lively and light shadows everywhere to accompany you in your meditation. As for when you are talking deeply with good friends and lovers, a candle is the best. Those dancing beautiful flames of candlelight have a rich life. The light and shadow it casts on objects are obviously different from the white-hot electric light. We no longer use candles, our ancient red candles, for anything other than worshiping gods, but I always love those two flickering little flames, smiling at you in a very kind and playful way, just like a pair of eyes that you are familiar with.

Let's not talk about the things about lamplight anymore. Although lamplight is lovely, the essence of night is not here. The infinite temptation of night is also not here. I am not a poet and cannot write out the mystery of night and all his stars, but the things inside are so 觉觉that even a poor collector like me will not be able to get any harvest.

You turn off the lamp and temporarily gaze at the window. If you are not familiar with the night, then your first surprise should be that what flows in from outside the window is not darkness, but a kind of gentle radiance, like a burst of light music, a洞洞箫xiao, a violin, or the singing of young women in a small garden. The lamplight disappears from your eyes, not extinguishing the light, but like falling a layer of curtain from your eyes, replaced by a deeper light. They first walk in lightly, as if afraid of disturbing the host, and then see that they can be received, and immediately walk all over the place with a gentle movement. They are so familiar with all things (because the emotion between the night and all living things is much deeper than that for people) that they immediately blend together. Night is the mother of all things, stroking them, comforting them, adding beautiful colors to them, eliminating all the scars they have suffered in life, and dressing them up to make them very beautiful things. In the gentle radiance of the night, ugliness is gone. The ordinary furniture in your room, the broken table, and the rusted wall are now appearing as pictures. Now they are all living things.

You temporarily gaze at the window. The radiance of the night flows into your eyes and into your heart. This will make you forget everything that happened during the day, whether it is joy or sorrow, and forget those things that urgently缠绕缠绕around you, such as social interaction, business, coping with the operation of daily life, etc. You temporarily think of nothing, making your heart pure white and flawless, capable of accommodating things that are deeper, more basic, and closer to your soul. Then, you will think of many, many emotions that have been deeply imprinted on your soul but have been covered by daily business. You will think of those big and small events that have equal印印

Autumn

— (Hua Photography)

Page 28

mark on the heart——a person who has loved with all their heart and soul, a sentence that falls on your heart, a gaze that has made contact with your eyes, or a flower bud with dew that you have secretly visited in the early morning, your heart can't help but throb, just like when you hesitate to say (I love you) to a little girl, or a silhouette that you have accidentally seen on the roadside, a lonely, happy,颓颓唐tang, beautiful silhouette, but later in your imagination, your soul裏裏grows and negotiates and becomes a familiar friend (the characters in dreams and imagination, like those in life, will change, grow, disappear, and die), or the story you wrote when you violently馳驰荡dang and used your blood and life to complete your ideals. These are things that you have long forgotten, but have not forgotten. Who can forget those things that have already made a mark on the soul, no matter how subtle they are? They are just resting in the depths of the heart, waiting for the right situation to reappear. These are led out by the tenderness of the quiet night, writing a smile or loneliness on your face, but whether it is a smile or loneliness, it is beautiful because it is涵涵育yu in the beauty of the night.

But don't always sit at the table, don't always沉沉in deep thought. Go and see the night again, throw yourself into the embrace of the night. First, go to the window, and a陈陈fresh breath will immediately blow on your face. Whether it is the coolness of summer or the cold of winter, it is suitable for you. Even in the cold winter, the night air will never make you uncomfortable. It is a very clear thing, like snowflakes falling on your palm. The cold stimulation can immediately make your spirit excited. You start to look outside, and you see that the colors and contours are melted together, forming a mysterious poetic tremor. Yes, in the radiance of the night, you can feel a kind of tremor, like what you feel on a琴琴弦xian that is emitting beautiful sounds. The shapes you see in the night are all active. They quietly travel, sing, and dance, transforming into infinite beauty, and this is a dark night without the moon, without the stars (you will feel more beauty in the night of the moon and stars). There are very few stars twinkle in the sky, which will move your eyes to raise to the sky, just encountering the light waves of the stars, just like you have encountered the light waves at the bottom of the eyes of a familiar and expectant eye. Dogs are叫叫calling in the distance, peaceful and gentle, crickets are singing a kind of song you have never known before near you, under the window. Light flows out of the distant windows like the radiance of gemstones, flowing coolness in summer and warmth in winter. Those lights are密密talking to you, telling you some light and beautiful words. At this time, ugliness, suffering, embarrassment, jealousy, hatred, and the sins of the world are temporarily eliminated. Your mood is beautiful, as beautiful as the night itself. Human beings are brothers, and human beings and all living things are brothers.

But you won't stay at the window for long. The night entices you to run into his complete embrace, to go to breathe the freshness of the night and throw yourself into the草草plants containing smiles. Then temporarily suspend this short article and wait for me to return to write it again. I believe it will be written better than it is now.

Youth Garden Submission Guidelines

(1) The text should focus on discussions of youth issues, news about domestic and foreign schools or students, essays, descriptions of school life, etc., and the style is not limited.

(2) The paintings should be limited to those about youth issues.
